## 词性 AUX (17 words)

- __be__: My name __is__ Richard Stewart. （2225 次） strong /biː/ （用来说明人、事物或状态，表示性质、状态、工作等） used to say something about a person, thing, or state, to show a permanent or temporary quality, state, job, etc.
- __do__: And where __do__ you live? （681 次） /də/ （与另一动词连用构成疑问句和否定句，包括表示禁止的命令，有时因文体原因亦可用于肯定句） used with another verb to form questions and negative sentences, including negative orders, and sometimes in affirmative sentences for reasons of style
- __will__: We__'ll__ be looking for your book. （397 次） /wɪl/ **将**，将要 used to talk about what is going to happen in the future, especially things that you are certain about or things that are planned
- __can__: __Can__ I help you? （211 次） strong /kæn/ **能**，会 to be able to
- __would__: __Would__ you like some coffee? （179 次） strong /wʊd/ （从过去的角度指将来发生的事）将，将要 used to refer to future time from the point of view of the past
- __could__: He couldn't take time off to come to New York with me. （62 次） strong /kʊd/ （can 的过去式，表示能够或允许）能，可以 past simple of "can", used to talk about what someone or something was able or allowed to do
- __should__: You __should__ take the number 1 subway. （46 次） strong /ʃʊd/ **应当**，应该 used to say or ask what is the correct or best thing to do
- __must__: And you __must__ be Susan. （31 次） strong /mʌst/ **必须** used to show that it is necessary or very important that something happens in the present or future
- __may__: __May__ I take a picture of you and your little boy? （19 次） /meɪ/ （表示可能性）可能，也许 used to express possibility
- __might__: It __might__ be a little cold. （17 次） /maɪt/ （may 的过去式）可能，可以 past simple of the verb may, used especially when reporting what someone has said, thought, asked, etc.
- __'ve(或许是 I've?)__: You must__'ve__ come home very late. （4 次）   
- __ought__: You really __ought__ to take some time off. （4 次） /ˈɔːt ˌtə/ （表示做某事有必要、值得或有利）应该，应当 used to show when it is necessary or would be a good thing to perform the activity referred to by the following verb
- __having__: Oh, I was sorry to hear about your wife __having__ passed away. （2 次） strong /hæv/ （与动词的过去分词连用，构成现在完成时和过去完成时） used with the past participle of other verbs to form the present perfect and past perfect
- __shall__: __Shall__ we go? （2 次） strong /ʃæl/ （用于在主语为 I 或 we 时替代 will） used instead of "will" when the subject is "I" or "we"
- __else'll(或许是 she'll?)__: Somebody __else'll__ buy it by then. （1 次）   
- __getting__: My niece is __getting__ married, and I've been trying to find just the right thing for her. （1 次） /ɡet/ **获得**，得到;买到;挣得，赢得 to obtain, buy, or earn something
- __helped__: Being with him __helped__. （1 次） /help/ **帮助**，帮忙 to make it possible or easier for someone to do something, by doing part of the work yourself or by providing advice, money, support, etc.

> be, do, will, can, would, could, should, must, may, might, ought, having, shall, getting, helped

## 词性 PART (3 words)

- __to__: Well, welcome __to__ New York. （1066 次） strong /tuː/ （用于动词前，表示不定式） used before a verb to show that it is in the infinitive
- __not__: Oh, it's __not__ finished yet, but I have some of the pictures. （508 次） /nɒt/ （用于 be，can，have，will，must 等动词后构成否定表达，在口语中常简略为n't）不 used to form a negative phrase after verbs like "be", "can", "have", "will", "must", etc., usually used in the short form "n't" in speech
- __'s(或许是 s?)__: Hold Gerald__'s__ hand, please. （109 次）   

> to, not

- __wash__: Well, in that case, you can __wash__ the dishes and clean up after dinner. （1 次） /wɒʃ/ **洗**，清洗，洗涤 to clean something using water
- __wound__: I've never seen you so __wound__ up. （1 次） /wuːnd/ （身体上的）伤，伤口 a damaged area of the body, such as a cut or hole in the skin or flesh made by a weapon
- __wrestle__: I've been __wrestling__ with the question of whether I go back to work or not. （1 次） /ˈres.əl/ （尤指作为运动）（与…）摔跤，角力;（将…）摔倒 to fight with someone (especially as a sport) by holding them and trying to throw them to the ground

## 词性 X (1 words)

- __DA__: __Da__ dada __da__ __da__ dada __da__ __da__ __da__ __da__ __da__ __da__ dada. （9 次） /ˌdiːˈeɪ/ **地方检察**官（district attorney的缩写） abbreviation for district attorney

## 句子
1. __Excuse__ me.
   - __excuse__ /ɪkˈskjuːz/ **原谅**;宽恕 to forgive someone or something (17 次)

2. I __call__ __it__ __Family__ __Album__, U.S.A. __Oh__, __that__'s a __nice__ __idea__.
   - __call__ /kɔːl/ **给…取名**，给…命名;称呼 to give someone or something a name, or to know or address someone by a particular name (78 次)
   - __it__ /ɪt/ （用作主语或宾语）它，这，那（指上文提到的事物、动物或情况） used as the subject of a verb, or the object of a verb or preposition, to refer to a thing, animal, situation, or idea that has already been mentioned (811 次)
   - __family__ /ˈfæm.əl.i/ **家**，家庭 a group of people who are related to each other, such as a mother, a father, and their children (88 次)
   - __album__ /ˈæl.bəm/ （CD或唱片上的）音乐专辑 a collection of several pieces of music, made available as a single item on a CD, the internet, etc. (12 次)
   - __oh__ /əʊ/ （表示惊讶、失望和高兴等情绪）噢，哎，唉，啊 used to express different emotions, such as surprise, disappointment, and pleasure, often as a reaction to something someone has said (215 次)
   - __that__ /ðæt/ **那**;那个;那人 used to refer to a person, object, idea, etc. that is separated from the speaker by space or time (383 次)
   - __nice__ /naɪs/ **愉快的**;美好的;满意的 pleasant, enjoyable, or satisfactory (73 次)
   - __idea__ /aɪˈdɪə/ **意见**，想法，主意;计划 a suggestion or plan for doing something (43 次)

3. __My__ __name__ is __Richard__ __Stewart__.
   - __my__ /maɪ/ **我的** of or belonging to me (= the speaker or writer) (296 次)
   - __name__ /neɪm/ **名字**，名称 the word or words that a person, thing, or place is known by (27 次)
   - __richard__    (121 次)
   - __stewart__    (129 次)

4. __May__ I __take__ a __picture__ __of__ __you__ __and__ __your__ __little__ __boy__?
   - __may__ /meɪ/ （表示可能性）可能，也许 used to express possibility (19 次)
   - __take__ /teɪk/ **拿**;夺取;取走 to remove something, especially without permission (111 次)
   - __picture__ /ˈpɪk.tʃər/ **画**，图画;照片 a drawing, painting, photograph, etc. (27 次)
   - __of__ weak /əv/ （用于表示归属或来历）…的，属于 used to show possession, belonging, or origin (402 次)
   - __you__ /juː/ **你**;您;你们 used to refer to the person or people being spoken or written to (1431 次)
   - __and__ strong /ænd/ （用于连接两个词、短语、句子成分或相关语句）和，及，又，并 used to join two words, phrases, parts of sentences, or related statements together (796 次)
   - __your__ strong /jɔːr/ **你的**;您的;你们的 belonging or relating to the person or group of people being spoken or written to (268 次)
   - __little__ /ˈlɪt.əl/ **小的**，少的 small in size or amount (52 次)
   - __boy__ /bɔɪ/ **男孩**;小伙子;男人，男子 a male child or, more generally, a male of any age (15 次)

5. __Now__ __point__ __to__ __the__ __buildings__.
   - __now__ /naʊ/ **现在**，此刻，目前 at the present time, not in the past or future (107 次)
   - __point__ /pɔɪnt/ **观点**;论点 an idea, opinion, or piece of information that is said or written (12 次)
   - __to__ strong /tuː/ （用于动词前，表示不定式） used before a verb to show that it is in the infinitive (1066 次)
   - __the__ strong /ðiː/ （用于名词前，指听者或读者已知的事物或人，尤指已提到的或能被领会的事物或人） used before nouns to refer to particular things or people that have already been talked about or are already known or that are in a situation where it is clear what is happening (1171 次)
   - __building__ /ˈbɪl.dɪŋ/ **建筑物**;房屋 a structure with walls and a roof, such as a house or factory (13 次)

6. __Well__, __welcome__ to __New__ __York__.
   - __well__ /wel/ **很好地**，令人满意地 in a good way, to a high or satisfactory standard (252 次)
   - __welcome__ /ˈwel.kəm/ **乐于接受**;欢迎;鼓励;支持 to be pleased about and encourage or support something (26 次)
   - __new__ /njuː/ **新出现的**;新兴的 recently created or having started to exist recently (79 次)
   - __york__ /jɔːk/ **约克** a city in northern England (30 次)

7. I'm a __photographer__.
   - __photographer__ /fəˈtɒɡ.rə.fər/ **摄影者**;摄影师 a person who takes photographs, either as a job or hobby (8 次)

8. __What__'s it __for__?
   - __what__ /wɒt/ **什么** used to ask for information about people or things (272 次)
   - __for__ strong /fɔːr/ （表示给予的对象）给 intended to be given to (382 次)

9. And __where__ __do__ you __live__?
   - __where__ /weər/ **去哪里**;在哪里 to, at, or in what place (37 次)
   - __do__ /də/ （与另一动词连用构成疑问句和否定句，包括表示禁止的命令，有时因文体原因亦可用于肯定句） used with another verb to form questions and negative sentences, including negative orders, and sometimes in affirmative sentences for reasons of style (681 次)
   - __live__ /lɪv/ **生存**;活着 (to continue) to be alive or have life (37 次)

10. Oh, it's __not__ __finished__ __yet__, __but__ I __have__ __some__ of the pictures.
    - __not__ /nɒt/ （用于 be，can，have，will，must 等动词后构成否定表达，在口语中常简略为n't）不 used to form a negative phrase after verbs like "be", "can", "have", "will", "must", etc., usually used in the short form "n't" in speech (508 次)
    - __finish__ /ˈfɪn.ɪʃ/ **完成**;（使）完结 to complete something or come to the end of an activity (18 次)
    - __yet__ /jet/ **还**，尚;迄今 still; until the present time (10 次)
    - __but__ strong /bʌt/ **但是**，不过;而;相反 used to introduce an added statement, usually something that is different from what you have said before (205 次)
    - __have__ strong /hæv/ （与动词的过去分词连用，构成现在完成时和过去完成时） used with the past participle of other verbs to form the present perfect and past perfect (531 次)
    - __some__ strong /sʌm/ **一些**，若干 an amount or number of something that is not stated or not known; a part of something (102 次)

11. __We__ live __in__ __California__.
    - __we__ strong /wiː/ （用作动词的主语）我们 used as the subject of a verb to refer to a group including the speaker and at least one other person (480 次)
    - __in__ /ɪn/ **在**（…）里面，在（…）内 inside a container, place, or area, or surrounded or closed off by something (347 次)
    - __california__ /ˌkæl.ɪ.ˈfɔː.ni.ə / **加利福尼**亚州（位于美国西海岸，首府为萨克拉门托，洛杉矶是其最大城市） a state on the west coast of the US, whose capital city is Sacramento and whose largest city is Los Angeles (2 次)

12. We'll be __looking__ for your __book__.
    - __look__ /lʊk/ **看**，瞧，注视 to direct your eyes in order to see (82 次)
    - __book__ /bʊk/ (纸版或电子版的)书 a written text that can be published in printed or electronic form (34 次)

13. __Great__!
    - __great__ /ɡreɪt/ **大量的**；巨大的；强烈的 large in amount, size, or degree (52 次)

14. __He__'s a __doctor__.
    - __he__ strong /hiː/ **他**（用于指代男人、男孩或雄性动物） used as the subject of a verb to refer to a man, boy, or male animal that has already been mentioned (319 次)
    - __doctor__ /ˈdɒk.tər/ **医生**，大夫 a person with a medical degree whose job is to treat people who are ill or hurt (13 次)

15. __Tell__ me __about__ your book.
    - __tell__ /tel/ **讲述**，说;告诉 to say something to someone, often giving them information or instructions (79 次)
    - __about__ /əˈbaʊt/ **在…方面**；有关，关于，涉及 on the subject of, or connected with (261 次)

16. Well, it's __fine__ __if__ you take __our__ picture.
    - __fine__ /faɪn/ **好的**;足够好的;健康的，身体好的 good or good enough; healthy and well (48 次)
    - __if__ /ɪf/ **假如**，如果 used to say that a particular thing can or will happen only after something else happens or becomes true (99 次)
    - __our__ /aʊər/ **我们的** of or belonging to us (71 次)

17. He __goes__ to __high__ __school__.
    - __go__ /ɡəʊ/ **去**;走 to travel or move to another place (250 次)
    - __high__ /haɪ/ （尤指无生命的东西）高的，有…高的 (especially of things that are not living) being a large distance from top to bottom or a long way above the ground, or having the stated distance from top to bottom (14 次)
    - __school__ /skuːl/ （中、小）学校 a place where children go to be educated (57 次)

18. __Would__ you __like__ some __coffee__?
    - __would__ strong /wʊd/ （从过去的角度指将来发生的事）将，将要 used to refer to future time from the point of view of the past (179 次)
    - __like__ /laɪk/ **喜欢**，喜爱 to enjoy or approve of something or someone (226 次)
    - __coffee__ /ˈkɒf.i/ **咖啡粉**;咖啡 a dark brown powder with a strong flavour and smell that is made by crushing dark beans from a tropical bush and used to make a drink (20 次)

19. Oh, __this__ is my __father__.
    - __this__ /ðɪs/ **这**，这个 used for a person, object, idea, etc. to show which one is referred to (226 次)
    - __father__ /ˈfɑː.ðər/ **父亲**，爸爸 a male parent (25 次)

20. I'm __sorry__ I'm __so__ __late__.
    - __sorry__ /ˈsɒr.i/ **悲伤的**，难过的;惋惜的 feeling sadness, sympathy, or disappointment, especially because something unpleasant has happened or been done (26 次)
    - __so__ /səʊ/ **很**，非常，这么，那么 very, extremely, or to such a degree (223 次)
    - __late__ /leɪt/ **末期的**，晚期的；接近终了 (happening or being) near the end of a period of time (27 次)

21. __With__ a Greek-__American__ family?
    - __with__ /wɪð/ **和…一起**；和；跟随；同 used to say that people or things are in a place together or are doing something together (221 次)
    - __american__ /əˈmer.ɪ.kən/ **美国的** of or relating to the United States of America (3 次)

22. __Good__-__bye__.
    - __good__ /ɡʊd/ **令人满意**的；令人愉快的；合意的；有趣的 very satisfactory, enjoyable, pleasant, or interesting (219 次)
    - __bye__ /baɪ/ **再见** goodbye (56 次)

23. __Thank__ you.

24. __Can__ I __help__ you?

25. __Let__ me __try__ it __on__.

    - __try__ /traɪ/ **试图**，想要；设法，努力 to attempt to do something (34 次)
    - __on__ /ɒn/ **在…上面**；到…上面 used to show that something is in a position above something else and touching it, or that something is moving into such a position (200 次)

26. And __these__ are pictures of __people__ __working__: steelworkers, bankers, police, __street__ vendors, ambulance drivers, doctors...
    - __these__ /ðiːz/ **这**，这些 plural of this (23 次)
    - __people__ /ˈpiː.pəl/ **人** men, women, and children (56 次)

    - __street__ /striːt/ **街**，街道，大街 a road in a city or town that has buildings that are usually close together along one or both sides (19 次)

27. Would you like to __see__ __them__?
    - __see__ /siː/ **看见**;看出 to be conscious of what is around you by using your eyes (134 次)
    - __they__ /ðeɪ/ （作主语）他们，她们，它们 used as the subject of a verb to refer to people, animals, or things already mentioned or, more generally, to a group of people not clearly described (192 次)

28. I've __got__ to go.
    - __get__ /ɡet/ **获得**，得到;买到;挣得，赢得 to obtain, buy, or earn something (186 次)

29. I __think__ it looks __terrific__ on you.
    - __think__ /θɪŋk/ **相信**;觉得;思考 to believe something or have an opinion or idea (183 次)
    - __terrific__ /təˈrɪf.ɪk/ **极好的** very good (20 次)

30. __She__ works for a __toy__ __company__.

31. I __know__.
    - __know__ /nəʊ/ **知道**，熟悉，了解 to have information in your mind (168 次)

32. __All__ __right__.

33. I was __expecting__ him __here__ __at__ __five__ __forty__-__five__.

    - __forty__ /ˈfɔː.ti/ （数字）40 the number 40 (10 次)

34. __Yes__.

35. Is __there__ a __station__ __near__ here?

36. __No__, I'm __from__ __Greece__.

    - __robbie__    (143 次)

40. __How__ __old__ are you, __Gerald__?

    - __gerald__    (6 次)

41. __Sure__, what do you __want__?

42. __OK__, __just__ a __second__.

43. __Hold__ Gerald's __hand__, __please__.
    - __hold__ /həʊld/ **握住**，抓住 to take and keep something in your hand or arms (15 次)
    - __hand__ /hænd/ **手** the part of the body at the end of the arm that is used for holding, moving, touching, and feeling things (7 次)

44. I'm taking __too__ __much__ of your __time__.
    - __too__ /tuː/ **太**；过于 more than is needed or wanted; more than is suitable or enough (94 次)
    - __much__ /mʌtʃ/ **多**（的），大量（的） a large amount or to a large degree (48 次)
    - __time__ /taɪm/ **时间** the part of existence that is measured in minutes, days, years, etc., or this process considered as a whole (105 次)

45. This is my __sister__ __Susan__.
    - __sister__ /ˈsɪs.tər/ **姐姐**，妹妹 a girl or woman who has the same parents as another person (4 次)
    - __susan__ /ˌleɪ.zi ˈsuː.zən/ **餐桌转盘**（餐桌上木质或塑料的圆盘，转动可使就餐的人都能取到食物） a circular piece of wood or plastic on a base that is put on a table and can be turned around so that everyone can reach the food that is on it (101 次)

46. __Hey__, let me take your picture!

47. It was a __pleasure__ __meeting__ you, too.
